MAINTANENCE AND INSURANCE CALCULATION FUNC

In [22]:
def get_yearly_costs(year_of_operation, purchase_cost):
    resale_value = cost_profiles.loc[cost_profiles['End of Year'] == year_of_operation, 'Resale Value %'].values[0] / 100
    insurance_cost = cost_profiles.loc[cost_profiles['End of Year'] == year_of_operation, 'Insurance Cost %'].values[0] / 100 * purchase_cost
    maintenance_cost = cost_profiles.loc[cost_profiles['End of Year'] == year_of_operation, 'Maintenance Cost %'].values[0] / 100 * purchase_cost
    return resale_value, insurance_cost, maintenance_cost

# Example for first 10 years
vehicle_costs = []
for index, row in vehicles.iterrows():
    for year in range(1, 11):
        resale_value, insurance_cost, maintenance_cost = get_yearly_costs(year, row['Cost ($)'])
        vehicle_costs.append({
            'ID': row['ID'],
            'Year': row['Year'] + year - 1,
            'Resale Value': resale_value * row['Cost ($)'],
            'Insurance Cost': insurance_cost,
            'Maintenance Cost': maintenance_cost
        })

vehicle_costs_df = pd.DataFrame(vehicle_costs)
print(vehicle_costs_df.head())

vehicles_fuel_costs['Fuel Cost'] = vehicles_fuel_costs['Consumption (unit_fuel/km)'] * vehicles_fuel_costs['Cost ($/unit_fuel)'] * vehicles_fuel_costs['Yearly range (km)']

# Function to calculate the total emissions for a given fleet composition
def calculate_total_emissions(fleet_composition):
    total_emissions = 0
    for vehicle_id, num_vehicles in fleet_composition.items():
        vehicle_emissions = vehicles_fuel_costs.loc[vehicles_fuel_costs['ID'] == vehicle_id, 'Carbon Emissions'].values[0]
        total_emissions += vehicle_emissions * num_vehicles
    return total_emissions

# Example fleet composition: {'BEV_S1_2023': 10, 'Diesel_S1_2023': 5}
fleet_composition = {'BEV_S1_2023': 10, 'Diesel_S1_2023': 5}
total_emissions = calculate_total_emissions(fleet_composition)
print(f'Total Carbon Emissions for the fleet: {total_emissions}')

Total Carbon Emissions for the fleet: 346739.8798128

CHECKING CONSTRAINS

In [27]:
def check_demand_satisfaction(fleet_composition):
    for year in demand['Year'].unique():
        for size in demand['Size'].unique():
            for distance in demand['Distance'].unique():
                required_distance = demand[(demand['Year'] == year) & (demand['Size'] == size) & (demand['Distance'] == distance)]['Demand (km)'].values[0]
                total_distance_covered = 0
                for vehicle_id, num_vehicles in fleet_composition.items():
                    vehicle_info = vehicles.loc[vehicles['ID'] == vehicle_id]
                    if vehicle_info['Size'].values[0] == size and vehicle_info['Distance'].values[0] == distance and vehicle_info['Year'].values[0] <= year:
                        yearly_range = vehicle_info['Yearly range (km)'].values[0]
                        total_distance_covered += yearly_range * num_vehicles
                if total_distance_covered < required_distance:
                    return False, f"Demand not satisfied for Year: {year}, Size: {size}, Distance: {distance}"
    return True, "Demand satisfied for all years, sizes, and distances"

# Example fleet composition
fleet_composition = {'BEV_S1_2023': 10, 'Diesel_S1_2023': 5}
demand_satisfied, message = check_demand_satisfaction(fleet_composition)
print(message)

Demand not satisfied for Year: 2023, Size: S1, Distance: D2
In [28]:
def check_emission_limits(fleet_composition):
    for year in carbon_emissions['Year'].unique():
        allowed_emissions = carbon_emissions[carbon_emissions['Year'] == year]['Carbon emission CO2/kg'].values[0]
        total_emissions = calculate_total_emissions(fleet_composition, year)
        if total_emissions > allowed_emissions:
            return False, f"Emission limit exceeded for Year: {year}"
    return True, "Emissions within limits for all years"

def calculate_total_emissions(fleet_composition, year):
    total_emissions = 0
    for vehicle_id, num_vehicles in fleet_composition.items():
        vehicle_info = vehicles_fuel_costs.loc[(vehicles_fuel_costs['ID'] == vehicle_id) & (vehicles_fuel_costs['Year'] <= year)]
        if not vehicle_info.empty:
            vehicle_emissions = vehicle_info['Carbon Emissions'].values[0]
            total_emissions += vehicle_emissions * num_vehicles
    return total_emissions

# Example fleet composition
fleet_composition = {'BEV_S1_2023': 10, 'Diesel_S1_2023': 5}
emissions_within_limits, message = check_emission_limits(fleet_composition)
print(message)

Emissions within limits for all years
In [29]:
def check_purchase_and_lifespan_constraints(fleet_composition):
    for vehicle_id, num_vehicles in fleet_composition.items():
        purchase_year = vehicles.loc[vehicles['ID'] == vehicle_id]['Year'].values[0]
        if vehicle_id in fleet_composition:
            if fleet_composition[vehicle_id]['purchase_year'] != purchase_year:
                return False, f"Vehicle {vehicle_id} purchased in incorrect year"
            if fleet_composition[vehicle_id]['purchase_year'] + 10 < current_year:
                return False, f"Vehicle {vehicle_id} exceeds lifespan"
    return True, "Purchase and lifespan constraints satisfied"

# Example fleet composition
fleet_composition = {'BEV_S1_2023': {'num_vehicles': 10, 'purchase_year': 2023}, 'Diesel_S1_2023': {'num_vehicles': 5, 'purchase_year': 2023}}
current_year = 2030
purchase_lifespan_valid, message = check_purchase_and_lifespan_constraints(fleet_composition)
print(message)

Purchase and lifespan constraints satisfied
In [30]:
def check_sales_constraints(fleet_composition):
    for vehicle_id, num_vehicles in fleet_composition.items():
        sales_count = fleet_composition[vehicle_id].get('sales', 0)
        total_fleet = fleet_composition[vehicle_id]['num_vehicles']
        if sales_count > 0.2 * total_fleet:
            return False, f"More than 20% of fleet {vehicle_id} sold in a year"
    return True, "Sales constraints satisfied"

# Example fleet composition with sales
fleet_composition = {'BEV_S1_2023': {'num_vehicles': 10, 'purchase_year': 2023, 'sales': 2}, 'Diesel_S1_2023': {'num_vehicles': 5, 'purchase_year': 2023, 'sales': 1}}
sales_valid, message = check_sales_constraints(fleet_composition)
print(message)

Sales constraints satisfied

OPTIMIZATION

In [35]:
import pandas as pd
import pulp



# Merge vehicles and vehicles_fuels on the ID column to get a complete view of each vehicle
vehicles_merged = pd.merge(vehicles, vehicles_fuels, on="ID")

# Initialize the problem
problem = pulp.LpProblem("Fleet_Optimization", pulp.LpMinimize)

# Decision variables: number of vehicles to buy, use, and sell
vehicle_ids = vehicles['ID'].unique()
years = range(2023, 2039)

# Dictionary to hold the decision variables
buy_vars = pulp.LpVariable.dicts("Buy", [(v, y) for v in vehicle_ids for y in years], lowBound=0, cat='Integer')
use_vars = pulp.LpVariable.dicts("Use", [(v, y) for v in vehicle_ids for y in years], lowBound=0, cat='Integer')
sell_vars = pulp.LpVariable.dicts("Sell", [(v, y) for v in vehicle_ids for y in years], lowBound=0, cat='Integer')

# Objective function: minimize total costs
total_cost = 0

for v in vehicle_ids:
    for y in years:
        vehicle_info = vehicles.loc[vehicles['ID'] == v]
        vehicle_fuel_info = vehicles_fuels.loc[vehicles_fuels['ID'] == v]

        # Skip if no matching rows found
        if vehicle_info.empty or vehicle_fuel_info.empty:
            print(f"Skipping vehicle {v} for year {y} due to missing data")
            continue

        # Accessing vehicle data
        vehicle_cost = vehicle_info['Cost ($)'].values[0]
        yearly_range = vehicle_info['Yearly range (km)'].values[0]

        # Calculate purchase cost
        purchase_cost = buy_vars[v, y] * vehicle_cost
        
        # Ensure the year_of_operation is within the range of cost_profiles
        year_of_operation = y - vehicle_info['Year'].values[0] + 1
        if year_of_operation <= 0 or year_of_operation > 10:
            continue
        
        # Calculate maintenance and insurance costs
        maintenance_cost_percent = cost_profiles.loc[cost_profiles['End of Year'] == year_of_operation, 'Maintenance Cost %'].values[0] / 100
        insurance_cost_percent = cost_profiles.loc[cost_profiles['End of Year'] == year_of_operation, 'Insurance Cost %'].values[0] / 100
        resale_value_percent = cost_profiles.loc[cost_profiles['End of Year'] == year_of_operation, 'Resale Value %'].values[0] / 100

        maintenance_cost = use_vars[v, y] * (maintenance_cost_percent * vehicle_cost)
        insurance_cost = use_vars[v, y] * (insurance_cost_percent * vehicle_cost)
        resale_value = sell_vars[v, y] * (resale_value_percent * vehicle_cost)

        # Accessing fuel data
        fuel_consumption = vehicle_fuel_info['Consumption (unit_fuel/km)'].values[0]
        fuel_type = vehicle_fuel_info['Fuel'].values[0]
        fuel_cost_per_unit = fuels.loc[(fuels['Fuel'] == fuel_type) & (fuels['Year'] == y), 'Cost ($/unit_fuel)']
        
        if fuel_cost_per_unit.empty:
            print(f"Skipping fuel cost calculation for vehicle {v} in year {y} due to missing fuel cost data")
            continue
        
        fuel_cost_per_unit = fuel_cost_per_unit.values[0]
        fuel_cost = use_vars[v, y] * yearly_range * fuel_consumption * fuel_cost_per_unit

        # Total cost for this vehicle and year
        total_cost += purchase_cost + maintenance_cost + insurance_cost + fuel_cost - resale_value

problem += total_cost
print(f"Objective function set with total cost: {total_cost}")

# Solve the problem
problem.solve()

# Print the status of the solution
print(f"Status: {pulp.LpStatus[problem.status]}")

# Print the optimal decision variables
for v in vehicle_ids:
    for y in years:
        if pulp.value(buy_vars[v, y]) > 0:
            print(f"Buy {pulp.value(buy_vars[v, y])} units of {v} in {y}")
        if pulp.value(use_vars[v, y]) > 0:
            print(f"Use {pulp.value(use_vars[v, y])} units of {v} in {y}")
        if pulp.value(sell_vars[v, y]) > 0:
            print(f"Sell {pulp.value(sell_vars[v, y])} units of {v} in {y}")

In [40]:
for v in vehicle_ids:
    purchase_year = vehicles.loc[vehicles['ID'] == v, 'Year'].values[0]
    lifespan = 10

    # Ensure vehicles are bought in the correct year
    problem += pulp.lpSum(buy_vars[v, y] for y in years if y != purchase_year) == 0

    # Ensure vehicles are used only within their lifespan
    for y in years:
        if y > purchase_year + lifespan:
            problem += use_vars[v, y] == 0

    # Ensure vehicles are sold after their lifespan
    for y in years:
        if y == purchase_year + lifespan:
            problem += sell_vars[v, y] == buy_vars[v, purchase_year]
In [41]:

        problem += sell_vars[v, year] <= 0.2 * pulp.lpSum(use_vars[v, y] for y in years if y <= year)

In [43]:
output_data = []

# Assuming you have a dictionary or similar structure with the optimization results
for v in vehicle_ids:
    for y in years:
        buy_qty = pulp.value(buy_vars[v, y])
        use_qty = pulp.value(use_vars[v, y])
        sell_qty = pulp.value(sell_vars[v, y])
        
        # Only add to output if there is a decision
        if buy_qty > 0:
            output_data.append([y, v, int(buy_qty), "Buy", None, None, None])
        if use_qty > 0:
            # Assume the distance_bucket and distance_per_vehicle are determined based on your model
            distance_bucket = vehicles.loc[vehicles['ID'] == v, 'Distance'].values[0]
            distance_per_vehicle = vehicles.loc[vehicles['ID'] == v, 'Yearly range (km)'].values[0]
            output_data.append([y, v, int(use_qty), "Use", vehicles_fuels.loc[vehicles_fuels['ID'] == v, 'Fuel'].values[0], distance_bucket, distance_per_vehicle])
        if sell_qty > 0:
            output_data.append([y, v, int(sell_qty), "Sell", None, None, None])
